# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="3497b-102">Membres obsolètes dans .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3497b-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3497b-103">Cet article répertorie les membres de type obsolètes dans .NET Framework 4,5 et versions ultérieures.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3497b-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3497b-104">Les membres de type sont regroupés par assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3497b-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3497b-105">Cet article ne liste pas les membres des types obsolètes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3497b-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3497b-106">Pour obtenir la liste des types obsolètes, consultez [types obsolètes](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3497b-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
